\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{integral_8h_source_l00811}00811 \textcolor{comment}{  /// 2D Gaussian integration class for linear triangles.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{integral_8h_source_l01228}01228 \textcolor{comment}{  /// 45 integration points. This integration scheme can}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{integral_8h_source_l01229}01229 \textcolor{comment}{  /// integrate up to eighth-\/order polynomials exactly and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{integral_8h_source_l01230}01230 \textcolor{comment}{  /// is therefore a suitable "{}full"{} integration scheme}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{integral_8h_source_l01231}01231 \textcolor{comment}{  /// for quartic elements in which the}}
